Desquelz li une maniere si est que tu faices III cauteres, ou IIII, en lignant selonc la longor de la mice, selonc la figure dou cautere dou foie que nos avons dit devant; et n’apresser mie ta main a tout le cautere, et soit li malaides sovins sor son dos; et une autre maniere de cautere si est que tu eschaufe le cautere qui a II ners, si com nos l’avons mostreit en la dislocation de l’espaule; et lieve le keur qui est endroit la mice, ou li coutes dou malaide vient devers senestre, et soit li elevations dont tu lieves le keur selonc la keur, selonc la longesce dou cors, et li cautere soient selonc la largesce dou cors.	One method involves making three or four cauterizations in a line following the length of the mouse, according to the shape of the liver cautery we described earlier; do not press your hand on the entire cautery, and have the patient lay prone on their back; another cauterization method is to heat the cautery with two nerves, as we showed for shoulder dislocation; lift up the heart which is towards the mouse, or where the pain of the patient originates from the left side, and make the elevation you use to lift the heart according to its core, following the length of the body, and let the cauterizations be made along the width of the body.
Aprés i boute les II ners enflamez tant que li keurs soit perciez de l’autre part, et puis trai fuers le cautere, et ensi en i avra IIII Et se tu vues, si cauterize a tot le cautere a III ners.	After inflating the two bladders so that the heart is pierced on the other side, then draw out the cautery, and thus there will be four of them. If you wish, cauterize the entire cautery with three bladders.
Aprés le cure quant il a geteit porriture par lonc tens, et ce vaut mues que li autre des cures devant dites.	After the treatment when there has been long-standing putrefaction, this is worth more than the other treatments mentioned above.
de ydropisie	Of hydropsy.
Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».	Cauterization is not beneficial for dropsy, except in the case of ascites.
Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis; et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur.	When you treat it according to the methods we have mentioned in the division and your treatment does not benefit them, then you must make four cauterizations around the navel, one on the stomach, one on the liver, one on the spleen, two behind the back over the spine, and one at the bottom; and let the cauterizations be close to the heart's point.
Aprés laisse le cautere aovert por giter porriture lonc tens, et ne lassier mie la cure dou malaide aprés le cautere; et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les II ententions avec l’aide de Deu.	After leave the cautery open to drain pus over a long time, and do not neglect the patient's care after the cautery; healing will be hastened, and the two intentions shall be together with God's help.
Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit; et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.	The shape of the cautery for the abdomen should be as we have shown before; and that for the back should be olive-shaped, according to what has been stated above.
de l’enfleure des piez	The swelling of the feet.
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire; et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	When the feet of one who is dropsical are swollen and filled with yellow water, it is necessary that you cauterize on the back of the foot between the little finger and ring finger; raise your hand with the cautery without turning it.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	And do not enter too deeply, otherwise you will injure the surrounding yellow tissue, and let the caustic be according to this form.
Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire; et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe; et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse; aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	After, make two cauteries on each leg at the tip of the shinbone; and let the caustics be in length, one below the knee in front and the other outside, in the middle of the leg; leave the cauterized area uncovered for a long time without cleaning, until the yellow tissue appears; after treating the other treatments that we have mentioned.
de la menoison	of the house
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures; et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule; et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.	When the purging of the belly comes from cold and moisture, so that the retaining and digestive virtues which are in the stomach and intestine are weakened, and cannot be treated by ordinary means; and you see the patient suffering greatly with strong constitution, then make one large cautery on the stomach according to what has been said before regarding the stomach cautery or circular cautery; four subtle cauteries around the navel each as thick as a small nail, and two cauteries on the hips.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et I cautere sus chaicun yle, et II petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	And if you see abundant moisture and the patient suffers, apply a fire cautery to the wrist, one cautery on each elbow, and two small cauteries near the large intestine, for treatment is beneficial when there is proper assistance.
de la cure des emorroydes	For the treatment of hemorrhoids.
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres: III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois; et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile; et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	When hemorrhoids are found in the anus, either one or more, and they are old and consist of cold, moist, corrupted humors, and treatment as previously mentioned has not worked, perform cauterization: three cauteries on the back spine, one each outside the armpits in a triangular pattern, and one cautery below the buttocks two fingers away; if you suspect their stomach is cooled and food is not being digested properly, and you observe swelling of the face, apply one large cautery to the stomach as previously mentioned, another on the liver, and another on the spleen with all cauteries clamped open for a long duration.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	After treatment, let the site heal until it is fully recovered.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	Of fleshiness which is named "thelul
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit; et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort; fai ceu une fois ou II, et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit; aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez; et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	When you treat thethelul, heat the cautery until it resembles a razor, and then place it fully heated onto the treated thethelul; leave your hand there until the cautery reaches the edge of the wound, from which blood will flow; do this once or twice, and if there is much thethelul, cauterize each one as we have said; afterwards treat with beneficial ointments until they are healed; and if you cauterize with a large cautery on alchatim, it will be of greater help.
de plaie mal curee	Of a wound poorly treated
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When the patient cannot endure cutting or opening, as we will describe in its place, such a sickness comes that can only be healed through cauterization.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	When anyone develops a fistula and it emits purulent and corrupted moisture, you must test it thoroughly with a subtle probe, and be mindful of the entire extent of the abscess.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing; et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	Heat the cautery until it seems like a razor, and insert it into the fistula according to how far the probe went in, and repeat the cauterization as many times as needed for the corrupted tissue to burn away; once, twice or thrice depending on the extent of the need; take care not to burn any nerves nor major veins.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans; aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement; et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font; et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	if the fistula goes into the body of the bladder and intestine, then be careful to protect those areas, and do not cauterize unless it is on fleshy ground, considering that this is a dangerous condition; after healing make sure you check if the wound has healed properly, and if the wound is salty or dry, and the matter has been removed for a long time, understand that the wound has completely healed; but if there remains some discharge, know that the wound is leaking and that the bone in the depths of its cavity is destroyed; this will be explained further later on.
de la maladie des reins	Of kidney disease: if it has not yet been pierced by an arrow, you should evacuate the urine in order to empty them entirely; but if they have been pierced already and discharge blood or pus, then treat as previously described for wounds caused by arrows.
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit; et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra III cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	When pain from coldness comes to the kidneys, along with severe flatulence and no sign of pregnancy, then you must perform a fire cautery on one side of the kidney, as well as the clavicle cauterization we previously described; and if instead, we cauterize in the middle point between both kidneys, there will be three cauterizations in line, which will provide greater benefit.
de la vessie	Of the bladder
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et I a destre et I a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce; et li fais I cautere defuers le dos, ou II se tu en as besoing; et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	When the bladder is soft and weak due to cold and moisture, causing the patient to retain urine, then cauterize in the area outside above the bladder, where the arm hair begins, on both right and left sides, each cautery should be as long as the width of a thumb; make one cautery outside the back, or two if necessary; the cauteries should be clamped according to the form previously described.
de la marris	Of the womb.
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde; et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor: adonques covient il c’on li faice III cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et II cauteres defuers le dos; et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	When the womb is cold and moist, preventing conception, and its flowers are corrupted with delayed termination; and when they come, she experiences great pain: then it must be done that three cauteries are made around the belly, as we have said for the bladder cautery, and two cauteries outside the back; the cauteries should be clamped, as we have said.
de la hainche	Of the hip
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble; et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a I cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle; et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	When the viscous moisture descends to the hip joint, and due to this it moves from its place, the sign is that one thigh appears longer than the other when measured together; and you will find the region of the pubic bone below, so you must cauterize the patient on the hip joint with I cautery similar to a circle, incising in front of the joint around the bone as it turns, ensuring the bone remains within the circle; and let the cauteries be like those used for stomach cautery.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai III cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs; et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if this cautery is not available to you, make three large olive-sized cauteries, and let the cauteries be as perfect as all hearts; treat until it is healed.
de la dolor de la hainche	Of the pain in the hip
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene: adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	When pain comes to the socket of the hip, caused by cold and moisture, and the patient is treated according to what we have said in the division but it does not heal, and the illness is chronic: then you must purge the patient of gross humors with foul-smelling pills or other good similar pills.
Aprés li fai cautere; et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres: c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	After that, apply cautery; and the manner of cauterization is of two kinds: namely, together with burning medicines, or cautery by fire.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz: que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire; aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	Cautery by fire has many methods, one of which is as follows: you cauterize over the socket of the hip with three triangular cauteries in this shape, making them deep and large, leaving between each cautery a space equal to the width of your thumb; make sure the cauteries are olive-shaped. Sometimes a cautery is made in the middle on top of the head of the hip, which means there will be four according to this shape:
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche; mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if you see fit, cauterize with the circular cautery that we mentioned before for the dislocation of the hip; but do so in such a way that the circles enclose the entire hip joint, and all the muscle tissue around the heart should be burned.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	This is how we proceed in cases of sciatica when the pain is localized to the hip and does not extend down into the thigh or leg.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc; et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur; et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	And if it extends down to the thigh and leg, apply two cauteries where the patient indicates the pain is located, and a third cautery above the ankle, slightly towards the left side. Let these be cup-shaped cauteries, burning through the muscle tissue around the heart; and should the patient feel that the pain reaches down to the sole of the foot or nearby, then cauterize where they indicate it hurts with three or four points using a sharp instrument known as a "point".
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus; et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	And if it is necessary, do more; and if you know that the pain is below the knee towards the thigh, then perform a cutellar or circular cauterization, and be careful in all your cauterizations not to leave the cautery for too long so as not to burn the nerves and large arteries, and not cause further harm and contraction to the patient.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	And I myself have seen many who were cauterized on the ankle of their foot, and it was left for so long that their leg became entirely swollen, as well as their foot, and all their feet were pierced and corrupted.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	After an abdominal operation which led to his death.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	And if the pain is in two connected parts, cauterize both of them in this way.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce; et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait; et c’est li forme:	And the wise men said regarding the cauterization of the hip joint, this is how it should be done: make such an iron tool and let its head be as big as a large navel orange or slightly smaller, and let there be slots between them with the width of one thumb each; and let these slots run through two sides, and also have notches like knots, and in the middle of it is a well-made piece of iron; and this is its shape:
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit; et lou cauterize une fois I cautere reont et lou laisse III jors; et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens; aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	Heated until it is all red and glowing, then place it on the sick hip joint, turning it over to the healthy side; cauterize once with this iron tool and leave for three days; afterwards apply a plaster of butter, and let the wound remain open for a long time; after curing with ointment until it has healed.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent; et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	Albucasim says that we use this cautery rarely due to the fear of its appearance, and few see it being used; yet, it is one of the good cauterizations, which can be endured by those who have it, and left where it hardens.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi; et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	The medicine cautery that burns is made with an instrument of interlaced rods where the edge of the door descends, and it should be made of brass or iron with one long side, and at a height of two inches; there should be a distance between each equal to the thickness of a finger; they are open from above and below, and join together in this shape:
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche; aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	Then place the wooden box of the hip on the patient lying on their healthy side, and quickly press your hand hard over the hip box; after that pour between the two circles some hot oil which has been heated a little by the fire, and leave it for an hour's time, enduring the heat and burning with the patient.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu; et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit; et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait; et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	For it is found there to be cauterization, as well as fire; and when the cauterization has passed, lift your hand with the instrument and gently raise the hip, and let it remain like this for three days, and apply butter until that which is black from the scald is removed; then leave it for another three days so that putrefaction is extracted; and this would be the last aid after the cure of ointments as long as it is healed.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument; et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	And if the pain has extended to the thigh or down to the leg, apply an instrument with gentle heat as you have done for the hip similarly; and this is the method of warm application, which I have written about in the treatise on medical corrections.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	Take alkali and quicklime, equal parts of each, grind them together, and place them in a new pot.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir; et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main; et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	where there is a small opening so that the tip of a razor can enter; place over it one pot or another well-plumbed pot, and put on alkali and heat and pour warm water above, until there are two fingers' depth above the powders when you have properly grasped it in your hand; leave it thus until cool water and liquid descend into the plumbed pot, then take all that liquid and pour it over heat and alkali as before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	and it will be very watery and administered in many medical practices and in cauterizing other members; for it does the same work as fire, and there are other medicines with which one can cauterize well the hip like these: theriac, honey of Anacardium, hot with soap, all these things mixed together.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	And Galen tells us of a cure where a man was healed from the pain in his hip and sciatic vein, and he praises it greatly, saying that no other treatment was needed, and that he was cured instantly when this cure was performed, and he bathed as he instructs hereafter.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie; et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	He says in this way that you should take fresh and dry green litharge, and grind it very well with one pound of grease, and apply it to the hip, thigh, and leg where the pain is located, and bind it; let it sit for three hours or however long it takes until the patient no longer feels the burning sensation.
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	Then have him enter the bath until his body is slightly moistened, and then put him to bed, and the pain will leave entirely and he will be healed.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	And know that no one should use such medicinal cauterization unless after evacuation from the body.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout; et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	And Dioscorides says that when the sciatic vein is cauterized with goat droppings, it greatly helps; and the cautery must be done in this manner.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	Take linen and smear it with old oil, and place it on the hollow area between the thumb of the foot and the other one called the fossa.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains; et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee; et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	After that, take dry goat droppings and ignite them until they become charcoal, then place it on the linen and leave it until it extinguishes; repeat this process again, and keep doing so without ceasing until you perceive through sensation that it has reached up to the hip, and that the pain has ceased; and this type of cautery is called "goat cautery".
de la dolor dou dos	Of the pain of the back
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back, whether due to falling or impact, excessive bleeding, cold matter spreading, in none of these cases are cauterizations effective except for those caused by the influx of cold matter.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir; et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»; et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	He must then be purged with foul-smelling pills or other similar remedies applied to the back where the pain is felt. Three lines of ink should be drawn there and in each line apply five cauterizations, varying according to his strength and endurance; and perform these cauterizations as follows for the type known as "points". If you wish, make three or four at the middle clavicle following this pattern:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor; et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	This illness often occurs in small children and the signs of its onset are narrow shoulders when they rise up and fear. You will find on the last vertebra of their back an appearance that spreads to the other vertebrae.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this one and wish to cure it, cauterize it with a hot iron according to this form.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	So that the cautery touches each part of the spine evenly.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	And if you wish to do so, cauterize around the spine with a sharp cautery in two or three lines, and let the points be close to each other.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	Afterward treat the place until it is healed according to what we have said, and beware that you do not bring a cautery on top of nerves in spasm.
de la dolor des jointes	On joint pain:
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere: fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	When joint pains are due to moist humors that spread throughout the body, and when it comes in feet, which doctors call "gout" properly, and when it is of cold nature and cannot be cured by medicine, then it should be treated with cautery in this way: make a lot of cauterizations around the ankle joint, and let the cauteries be olive-shaped according to this form:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	And if there is a need for you to grasp onto the face of the foot, let it be cauterized completely with what we call "the point" cautery.
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire; et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	If the pains extend to the knees and other joints, and this happens often, apply three or four cauterizations on each knee, using the "olive" cautery; if more is needed, do more but do not hold your hand over the area for longer than it takes for the heartwood of the stake to burn.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	And if the pains descend to the knees and back, administer the cautery as we have described in this chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes; et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main; et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	If the pains are in the hands, make two lines of points around the knuckles; if there is any remaining pain in the fingers, make points on each joint and on the hair of the hand; if the pains extend to the wrists or shoulders, cauterize each affected area, and ensure proper care for the patient and provide medications.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	For if you give him good treatment and purge his phlegm, he will recover with God's help.
de la routure dou syfac	Of the fracture of the thighbone.
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor; et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre; aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors; puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	When fracture occurs in the thigh and the balls descend into the testicles, if it is recent, you should ensure that he does not eat on that day; and have him use things that empty the stomach so that feces leave his belly; afterward make him lie on his back between your hands, tell him to hold his breath until the balls return to their place, then bring them back with your two hands and cauterize below the fracture over the hip bone, and wherever there is a sign like half a circle above the body; then heat up this type of cautery:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	As long as they are white and emit no odor.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu; et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier; et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains; puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os; et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere; que tu ne le brulasses; et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	Pull the balls back to their place; and let your assistant hold his hand there so that it does not return backwards; and work well on the patient's thighs, placing a pillow beneath him with another one under the thighs, along with another holding the hands; then put the cautery onto the sign for as long as you have control over your own hand, and hold it straight and keep it in place until you reach the bone, if you do not reach that point on the first time, try again another time until you reach the bone. Be careful to avoid letting the balls move when performing the cautery, or burn them; lest the patient dies, or some other bad thing happens.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	And know that if you do not reach the bone with your cautery, then your work is worthless.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure; aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee; aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee; et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	And the cauterization for children should be done with subtlety according to their size, and for adults it should also be proportionate to their size; after three days treat the area with butter until the burning sensation is gone; after that apply other ointments until it is healed, and have the patient lie on his back for forty days until the wound is fully closed; and make sure their nourishment is sufficient so that their mouth doesn't dry out when they try to get up and walk.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors; et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire; et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	After forty days, when he wishes to get up, provide him with a well-made bandage, and let him wear it for another forty days; ensure he gets good rest, that he doesn't overwork himself, and guards against excessive fullness from drinking and eating, and against too much shouting; once he follows this guidance, he will be completely healed.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	And I will now describe the treatment for amputation in this chapter.
de la routure dou ventre	Of abdominal rupture.
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur; aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit; et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	When ruptures occur in other abdomens and are evident, and you see that they no longer grow, if it requires a caustic treatment according to its quantity, and the third part of the heart is burnt; after this treatment as we have said; and some ancients say it must be cauterized with a three-angled cautery in this shape:
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	But first mark the place of the wound and draw a line across the width above the rupture, then another outside it, and hold your hand steady throughout while using the cautery.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	But the first cauterizations are lighter and milder.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	of old pain in any limb
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	When pain arises in any limb, whether from falling or injury, and this pain persists for a long time, and medical treatment is ineffective, then it must be cauterized with the cautery called 'point', and the cauterization should be according to the length of the limb, its thickness, weakness, strength, location of torsion, and the intensity of the pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien; se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	If the first cauterization is effective, that's good; if not, apply another cautery over the previous one, as it is customary for it to affect the adjacent limb, therefore you must perform cauterizations until the patient is cured.
de meselerie	of surgery
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	The months are aided sometimes by cautery with great help, especially for illnesses that come from the putrefaction of phlegm and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief: I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous; et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel; et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir; et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	If you want to see the patient cauterized, be mindful if they are still in the early stages of illness and have been treated according to what we said before about division, and do not descend nor remain there, but you doubt that corruption will affect the whole body, then make five cauterizations on their head: one in the middle of the head at nine centimeters, another towards the front at the end of the hair; two on both corners, and one behind on the nape; leave your hand there until the cautery reaches the bone, and until scabs come out so that the vapors from thick humors can escape; then cauterize over the eye according to what is previously stated.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse; et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules; et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains; et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler; et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	Et si la blessure est partout dispersée ; elle perd manifestement, alors il faut que tu le cautérises avec ces cautères que nous avons dit sur le crâne, et un cautère sous le nez, deux cautères sur la colonne vertébrale du cou, six cautères sur la colonne vertébrale du dos, un grand cautère sur la croupe et un autre à côté, deux sur les deux épaules ; deux sur les coudes, deux sur les tendons de l'épaule, un sur chaque articulation des mains et des pieds, et sur les creux des mains ; fais attention aux nerfs qui sont situés derrière le talon, pour ne pas les brûler ; et parfois fait un cautère sur l'os du poignet, un autre sur l'os de l'estomac, et un autre sur le foie.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite; et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	Et sache qu'autant tu en fais de plus de cautère, autant tu lui apportes d'aide et plus cela lui profite ; et sache que les malades ne ressentent pas de douleur au cautère comme les sains le ressentent, car leur corps est déjà tout corrompu.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	And it is necessary that the cautery be large and small according to the limbs and joints, depending on what you find suitable in terms of iron instruments.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	After treatment, dress the wound with flour paste mixed with honey and other remedies until it is healthy.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre; et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur; puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	When swelling occurs in any limb and is treated with medicines, oils, and poultices, but it does not heal, then make cautery marks on the limb according to its size, slightly penetrating into the flesh; let the cautery be a little closer to the heart; then treat it with ointments until it is healed.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure; et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	And sometimes cautery is done on the hand, foot, or back, at the exit point of a nerve that moves the limb, and in this way, the swelling is removed; however, no one should intervene unless they are knowledgeable about limbs and the pathways of nerves moving through the body.
de albaras	Of scurvy
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color; puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie; et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	When the disease called "scurvy" is persistent, and medicinal remedies are ineffective, then cauterize it with a perfect cautery, according to the species of heart, until the whiteness is removed, and its color changes; then treat it with a mixture of flour from vetch and lentils, rose oil, plantain leaves, partridge blood, and pigeon's blood; blend all together, bind it with a piece of cloth, and expose it to air until it heals.
li cure de chancre par cautere	The treatment of cancer by cautery.
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	When cancer appears at its beginning, and you wish to halt its progress, cauterize it with a circular-shaped cautery tool, all around the cancerous growth.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre; et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois; et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	And yet the wise say that a cauterization should also be done in the middle of the chancre; and yet this does not seem good to me, for I fear it may become ulcerated and corrupted, and I have already seen this happen once; and a more proper thing is for it to be cauterized around, with the cautery called "circular", as we have said much about cauteries.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	Of the swelling that cannot die
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens; et tu la vues haster de meurer: adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant; aprés le laisse ensi.	When someone has an illness called "adubelati", and it delays death due to its nature or the excessiveness of its symptoms, or because of the patient's condition when he is decrepit (that is, very old) and has little blood, or due to the season; and you see that it hastens his death: then cauterize them around with many small cauteries while pricking; afterwards leave him be.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	For she will hasten to die.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you see it piercing through at all the cautery site, then heat up the cautery with what it is formed from here:
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	And place your hand in the middle of this illness called "adubelati" until the cautery site has pierced through the heart, and make sure that the cauterization is such that the patient feels it externally so that the course of putrefaction is alleviated.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	After treatment, wait until it is perfectly healed.
li cure dou feu par fer	The iron fire treatment
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	There is another kind of illness which is called "corrodens", and it is nothing other than the wasting away of limbs, for it eats away at the limbs just as fire consumes dry wood.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est; aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	If you see this illness in a place that can bear the fire cautery, then heat up small and large clavicle-shaped cauteries, according to what is suitable for the location where the illness is; afterwards cauterize it from all sides so much that you eradicate all corruption, and leave nothing of it behind, so that everything that is corrupt is removed.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	Leave it for three days, and then apply on the cauterized spots a soft ointment with oil so that the scabs from the fire are removed, along with all the corruption.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	Afterwards treat the resulting wound with ointments which produce flesh.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin; et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	And if you see after three days that healthy flesh has not grown, it is good; and if it hasn't, then begin the cauterization again on what remains of the corrupted spots.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu; mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division: pren la quant tu en as mestier.	And this treatment was sometimes cured by medication instead of fire cautery; however, fire cautery is still more effective and helpful, and I have already mentioned the cure with medication in the previous section: take it when you need to.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	For corns that come on the feet
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	Many times there is a disease that arises on the feet due to an external cause which we call 'corns', and it is a faulty, swollen thing that wounds the foot.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	And the treatment of this disease is according to two methods.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	That is to say fire cautery, and hot water cautery.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges; aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou; et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture; puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	Cautery of fire is when you heat a cauterizer shaped like an arrowhead made of good iron to fit the nail tightly and with fine margins; after putting it hot on the nail, turn your hand all around the nail until it reaches the bottom; leave it there for three days until it begins to discharge pus; then make a poultice of wild mallows crushed with salt and let the poultice stay overnight, the nail will fall out and be uprooted.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat the wound with ointment until it heals properly.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude; et est en teil maniere: pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues; et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine; et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre; puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	And if they are converted by fire in the body and happen often on hands and feet, you must apply hot water cauterization to them. It is done like this: take a cane of copper or iron, or an arrowhead, and put it on the nail and wart; that is for warts with a nail; and place the cane so it embraces everything around, then pour some hot water onto it, hold your hand steady, and press your hand turning so the margin of the cane reaches the root of the nail, and let the hot water go deep down to the root. Let the patient endure the burning sensation of the hot water for an hour; then leave it be, and all will get uprooted from their roots.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	Thus do one after another until you eradicate all those that are in the body, then treat them with ointments that produce flesh.
li cure dou trembler	The treatment for shaking/trembling.
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee; et I cautere ou pez, et I sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire; si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	When some shake due to coldness of nerves, or quartan fever or other, you must apply four cauterizations on the spine of the back, one between each vertebra; one cautery on the foot, and one on the stomach using the olive [shaped] cautery; this will stop the shaking and hasten recovery from the cold disease.
des pustules puans	Pustules that stink.
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	Sometimes certain bodies are covered in scabs or stinking pustules that come from gross corrupt matter.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule: un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	so it is fitting in the first instance when they appear that one perform a cautery on each head of the pimple: a subtle cautery with myrtle wood, whose point has been heated over fire, or with the root of long aristoloche, or with a lenticular cauterizer.
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez; mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	And one must cauterize them at the beginning when they appear according to this method, and they cannot grow any further, but rather the excess from which it comes is destroyed, and they are healed; however, it should be done after the evacuation of blood.
quant li artere est copee	when the artery is cut
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses; et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	There are often great outpourings of blood from the artery which is cut in the wound that comes afterwards, or in the incision of the abscess, or to cauterize a limb, and similar things; and it is very difficult to stop this bleeding.
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus; puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge; puis empren I, ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	And yet when this happens to someone, you must hurry to place your index finger on the wound's injury, and press down so that blood is calmed beneath your finger, and no more drops come out; then take many small and large olive oil cauterizers until they are all red hot; then take one, big or small according to the wound and the area where the artery is located, and place the cauterizer on that vein where you hold your finger, and keep it there until the blood is staunched.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement I autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	And if blood spurts forth when you lift your finger from the wound, and the first cauterizer is extinguished, then quickly take another one of the cauterizers that are on the fire.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez; et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide; et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des IIII manieres que nos avons dit: ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc; et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	Do not cease to do this one after the other until the blood is completely staunched; and make sure that you do not burn the nerve nearby, and that no other harm comes upon the patient; and know that when blood pours from an artery, it cannot be properly staunches unless by one of four methods we have mentioned: either by cauterization, or by extraction if it has not been treated already, or by very tight binding with thread, or by medicines placed on it which have the power to staunch blood; and ensure that the patient is bound firmly.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	Whoever brings restraint with narrow bandages or applies hot compresses of cloth, or other similar things, it is not beneficial if there are no improvements.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne; et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez; et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	And if this happens to anyone and there is neither physician nor medicine present, one must place their index finger on the wound of the vein as we have said before, and stretch it until it is constricted over the wound and over the vein; do not move the finger, but moisten it with cold water often so that it is very cold to freeze and swell the blood and constrict it; and make preparations beforehand for what is needed of cauterization and medicines.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	Here begins the second book on surgical treatments.
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres; et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.	We have told you in the first chapter all about diseases that require fire cauterization or burning medicines, and the instruments and methods of cauterization; I placed this chapter on the head down to the feet, and I will follow the same path in this chapter so that what one seeks is found more easily.
Et ainsois que je encomence ceu, il covient, chier fil, que vos aprenez que en cest chapistre a plus de peril et de paor que ou premier des cauteres, et por ceu il covient plus grant cautele.	And so when I begin this work, it is necessary, dear son, for you to learn that in this chapter there is more danger and fear than in the first about cauterization, and thus greater caution is required.
Car en l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’incision sus aposteme, et as cures des plaies, et a l’estraction des saiettes, et a l’incision sus la piere, et les semblans choses; ou il a doutance et paor, et en vient li mors a plusors.	For in the work of this chapter, there is often the evacuation of blood when opening a vein, and incising an abscess, and in the treatment of wounds, and in the extraction of arrows, and in cutting into stones, and similar things; where there is doubt and fear, and many die.
Et je vos amoneste que vos n’entreprenez folie.	And I warn you not to undertake this foolishly.
Car mout de manieres de gens vienent en cures.	For many types of people come for treatment.
si vienent de telz qui s’aïrent si avec lor maladie qu’il muerent legierement por la forsenerie qu’il trueve de sa maladie, et de la grandour de son malice; et de ces doit on avoir paor.	If they come from such people who are so afraid of their illness that they die quickly due to the frenzy caused by their disease and the severity of their condition, one should have fear.
Et de ces i a qui te done son sens, et dit: «atendez, je sui garis»; et li maladie est despitouse.	And there are those who show you their improvement, saying, "Wait, I am cured"; but the illness is malicious.
Il ne covient mie que vos vos consentez a ces qui vienent a vos qui ont ceste maniere, mais mettez plus grant cusanson en vostre honor qu’en vostre covoitise, et n’ovrez mie folement mais saigement de ceu dont vos estes certain, et dont vos poez avoir pris et los; et usez de pronostication et de indication en cures de vos malaides a coi salus soit convertie; et ceu vos aidera a aquester bone renommee, et gloire, et memoire de loenge.	You should not consent to those who come to you with such an attitude, but place greater concern for your honor than for your greed, and do not work foolishly but wisely on what you are certain of and can achieve results from; use prognostication and indication in the treatment of your patients towards which healing may be directed; this will help you gain a good reputation, glory, and a memorable legacy.
Tres chier fil, Nostres Sires vos doint boin entendement et droiture, et se vos vuelle espireir de la sainte inspiration de sa main, amen.	Tres chier fil, Our Lord give you good understanding and righteousness, and may he breathe into you the holy inspiration of his hand, amen.
Or je vos ai ordeneit cest chapistre en devisant par chapistres, selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre des cauteres, que je vos ai deviseit des le chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que vos trovez plus legierement ceu dont vos avrez mestier.	Or I have ordered this chapter to be divided into chapters, according to what is presented before in the chapter on cauterization, which I explained to you from head to toe so that you may find more easily what you need.
dou chief plein d’aigue	head full of water
Saiches que ceste maladie vient mout de fois as enfans a l’enfanter, et quant li baille estraint trop fort le chief de l’enfant; et aucune fois vient ceu de cause reponue que on ne seit.	Know that this illness often comes to children during birth when the midwife squeezes too hard on the child's head, and sometimes it has unknown causes.
Et je ne vis onques ceste maladie fuers qu’en enfans, et a toz ces que j’ai veus se hastait li mors; et por ceu me semble qu’il me vaut mues lassier l’ovraige en teilz cures.	And I have never seen this illness occur in anyone but children, and death was swift for all those whom I saw afflicted by it, so I think it best to leave aside such treatments.
Et je vis I enfant de coi li chiés estoit plains d’aigue, et li chief engroissoit chescun jor tant qu’il ne lou pooit sostenir; et crut tant li moistor qu’il fut mors, et ceste moistor si est assemblee desoz l’os sus lou syphac, entre lou keur et l’os; et li ovraiges si est telz se li moistor est entre lou keur et l’os, et li apostemes est petis, que tu fendes emmi lou chief une fendure large; et soit ausi longe com II nous, tant que li mostor corre; et vez ci la forme dou spatumile:	And I saw a child whose shoulder was full of fluid, and the head grew larger each day until he could no longer bear it; the moisture increased so much that he died, and this moisture had gathered beneath the bone on the scapula, between the heart and the bone; if the moisture is between the heart and the bone, and the abscesses are small, then you should make an incision in the head as wide as two fingers; let it be as long as two inches, so that the moisture flows out; here is the form of the spatulum:
Se li moistor est plus creue, et li aposteme soit plus grans, si fai II fendures en maniere d’une croix, selonc ceste forme:	If the moisture is deeper, and the abscesses are larger, then make two incisions in the form of a cross, according to this shape:
Et se li moistor est desoz l’os, et li signes que tu vois les commissures dou chief overtes de chescune partie, et li aigue saut fuer quant tu la presses de ta main au dedens, et ceu ne t’est mie reponut: si covient que tu fendes enmi lou chief III fendures selonc ceste maniere:	And if the moisture is beneath the bone, and you see that the sutures of the head are open on each side, and the fluid gushes out when you press it with your hand inside, and it does not stop, then you must make three incisions in the head according to this manner:
Et aprés l’incision estrai la moistor toute fuers.	And after the incision, remove all moisture immediately.
Aprés estraint les fendures de drapelz et de poudres, et i met vin et oile, et laisse ensi jusc’a cinquieme jor; puis le deslie, et cure la plaie par tentes et par oignemens, et laisse estraindre le chief egaument, et done mengier au malaide viande seche de poc de moistor tant que li membre soit confortez et sanez.	After applying compresses and powders, bind it with wine and oil, and leave it thus for five days; then untie it, and treat the wound with dressings and ointments, leaving the head immobilized equally, and feed the patient dry meat without moisture until the limb is strengthened and healed.
Et une autre maniere d’incision est que tu regardes ou apert li grandor de l’aposteme, et li assemblé de l’aigue; car aucune fois est elle devant; aucune fois derrier; aucune fois en destre; et aucune fois en senestre.	And another way of incision is to observe where the swelling of the abscess appears, and the accumulation of pus; for it may be in front, behind, on the right, or on the left side.
Taille donques lai ou li aposteme apert, et l’emplissement de l’aigue, et lou fent selonc ce que tu en as le pooir; et warde que tu ne coper l’artere; et veigne flun de sanc, si que li malaides muere dou decorrement de sanc et de l’evacuation de moistor.	Therefore, cut there where the abscess appears, and incise it according to its size and depth; be careful not to sever an artery, and expect blood flow, so that the patient does not die from excessive bleeding and moisture loss.
de reume	Of rheumatism
Quant il avient a aucun une maladie qui est apelee «catarre» as eulz ou au pis, et li maladie est anciainne, et li cure de medicine ne profite mie, adonques li derraine cure si est li cauteres avec ceu c’on li copera les II arteres.	When someone has a disease called "cataract" in the eyes or throat, and it is an old illness that does not respond to medical treatment, then the last resort is cauterization along with the cutting of the two arteries.
Il covient donques, cant tu les vues coper, que li malaides faice rere son chief; aprés li frotte lou leu d’un drapel aspre tant que les arteres aperent, puis estraingne li malaides son col a tout I drapel; puis regarde ou li voine bait, et li leus de l’une et de l’autre sont aprés les oreilles, et poc sont reponues; puis signe les leus d’enche, puis cope l’une et l’autre d’un spatumile agut de II pars, tant que li taille veigne jusc’a l’os, et ceu soit par lou large dou chief.	You must therefore, when you cut the veins, have the patient bend their head back; afterward, rub the place with a rough cloth until the arteries appear, then strap the patient's neck tight with a piece of cloth; then look where the vein beats, and the holes on either side are behind the ears, and they respond quickly; then mark these spots with your finger, then cut both of them with a sharp spatula in two movements, so that the incision reaches down to the bone, and this is done from the wide part of the head.
Et se tu vues, boute le spatumile desoz l’artere et la cope au desus, en taillant ausi com II dois au traver.	And if you see it, push the spatula under the artery and cover it above, cutting through as deeply as necessary for length two.
Et quant li voinne est copee, si saut li sans en haut continuelment fuers.	And when the vein is opened, blood flows continually out of it upwards.
Et se li artere n’apert au sentir, si covient que tu mesures la quantiteit de l’espaice de III dois, puis seigne d’enche et fent jusc’a l’os; et ceu qu’il covient dou sanc mettre fuers si est VI c/, et par aventure un poc plus ou moins, selonc ce que li malaides puet soffrir, et la repletion de l’artere; puis regarde la plaie: s’il remaint sus l’os point dou syphac, si le cope que apostemes chaus n’i veigne, puis estrain la plaie et lie, et la cure d’oignement tant qu’ele soit sanee.	If the artery does not open to the touch, you must measure the space of three fingers and then make an incision up to the bone; what needs to be released from blood is six half-fingers, and maybe a little more or less depending on how much the patient can endure and according to the fullness of the artery; then observe the wound: if it remains above the bone without a seal, cauterize so that no abscess comes, then extract the wound and bind it, treating with ointment until it is healed.
de emigrainne	Of migraine
Quant emigrainne anciaine vient, et catarre agut, por les moistors des larmes et les chalors en temples et sode anciene forsenee et semblans choses, et il est medicinez par manieres de cures de medicine et tout ceu ne li profite mie, si estraions les arteres des temples et lou cauterizons, si com nos avons conteit.	When an old migraine comes with acute catarrh due to the moisture of tears and heat in the temples, along with chronic headaches and similar issues, and all medicinal treatments are ineffective; we extract the arteries from the temples and cauterize them, as we have described.
Et li maniere de l’estraction d’elles si est que li malaides faice rere les poilz de ses temples, et entende a l’artere qui apert en la temple, car elle apert bien par son batement, et est poc reponue fuers que en aucuns homes qui sont trop froit; et s’elle est reponue, si estraigne son col li malaides d’aucuns drapelz, puis frote le leu d’aucun aspre drap, et arose le leu d’aigue chaude tant que li artere apere manifestement; puis pren le spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	And the method of extraction is as follows: The patient should shave their hair from the temples and pay attention to the artery that appears in the temple, for it can be easily seen by its pulse, especially if it is close to the surface except in some individuals who are very cold; if it is deep, then the patient should tighten their neck with some cloths, then rub the area with a rough cloth and warm water until the artery becomes clearly visible; then take the spatule which has this shape:
puis escorche le cuir legierement tant que tu veignes a l’artere, puis la trai en haut as pinceures, et la depart bien des toiles que sont desoz li de chescune partie; et se li artere est subtilz, si la torne a la pointe de l’uncine, puis la cope de celle partie selonc la quantiteit des II chiés.	Then scrape the skin lightly until you reach the artery, then pull it upwards with pincers, and separate well the membranes that are beneath each part; and if the artery is delicate, turn it to the tip of the hook, then cut off that part according to the size of II fingers.
Car s’elle n’est copee, si ne saut mie li sans dou tout en tout.	For if it is not cut off, blood cannot flow through fully.
Et trai dou sanc des VI c/, jusc’a III; et se li artere est grans, si covient que tu la lies en II leus d’un fil double fort de soie, que porriture n’i veigne devant le soudement de la plaie, et veigne decorremens de sanc; puis cope la superfluiteit qui est entre les II liiens en celle houre meisme, et puis, se tu vues, si lou cauterize dou cautere cutellaire jusc’a l’os tant que li chiés soient copez; et c’est li muedre oevre, se li malaides n’a fievre et il est de chaude complexion.	And draw out the blood from the six parts down to three, and if the artery is large, you must tie it in two places with a strong double silk thread, so that gangrene does not come before the wound heals, and bleeding continues; then cut off the superfluity which is between the two ties at that very moment, and then, if you wish, cauterize it with a knife down to the bone until the fingers are cut off; this is a dangerous operation, if the patient has no fever and is of warm complexion.
Car li cauteres est aide por finir les moistors: por ceu est il de plus grant aide as moistors.	For cauterization is a help to dry out moisture; therefore, it is of great assistance for moisture-related issues.
Ou il covient por l’estraction des arteres que om emplisse lou leu de viel coton et mette on sus tentes bien faites; et quant on les desliera, si soit curez de medicines seches que font naistre char, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez; et se sans cort de l’artere tant dis com tu i oevres, si te haste dou coper par cautere, ou tu emple lou leu de vitriole et l’estrain a ta main que li sans soit estainchiez; et se tu n’as ceu present, si met sor le leu ton doit tant que li sans soit congelez, et arose le leu d’aigue froide tant que li sans cesse, et soit estraint si com il covient; et ceu qui est muedre et plus legier en l’estraction de l’artere est que tu cauterizes la voinne de cest cautere trenchant de II pars, mais li trenchant soient bien espés por warder plus longement lor chalor.	Where it is necessary for the extraction of arteries, one should fill the space with old cotton and place well-made bandages on top; and when you release them, ensure that they are treated with dry medicinal substances that promote flesh growth, and with bandages, until they are healed; and if there is an accidental cut from the artery while you work, then quickly perform a cauterization or use vitriol and extract it by hand to stop the bleeding; and if you do not have these things present, then put your finger on it until the blood is frozen, and pour cold water over the area until the bleeding stops, and ensure that it is tightly bound as necessary; and what is important and lighter in terms of artery extraction is that you cauterize the vein with this trenchant cautery in two parts, but let the incisions be well spaced to maintain its heat for longer.
Car quant li estrumens est trop tenves, si tient moins sa chalor.	For when the instruments are too thin, they hold less heat.
Et doit avoir entre les II coutelz I doit de gros d’espaice, et puis quant tu as signiet d’enche les II leus, et tu mes lou fer ardant sus tant qu’il viegne jusc’a l’os, et cope la voinne en II leus; et soient esloigniet entre les II chiés car il n’est mie soudez de cest cautere dou tout en tout; et c’est li forme dou cautere:	And it must have a gap of about an inch between the two blades, and then when you have struck to enter the two places, place the burning iron upon it until it reaches the bone, and cut the vein into two parts; let them be separated between the two shoulders for they are not completely joined in this cauterization from end to end; and this is the shape of the cautery:
des larmes	tears.
Quant les larmes des eulz sont dessendans des voinnes que sont sus lou test dou chief de fuer, et il ne profite mie cure de medicine c’on i faice, et tu vois la faice dou malaide enrougir, et sent ou front ambulation si com de fremis; et sui oil sont tenve et moiste si que li poil des papieres sont cheut, et sont eschaufees les papieres, et escorchies de l’ardor des larmes, si ait mestier de ceste cure.	When the tears from the eyes flow down the veins that are on top of the skull, and no medicine cures it, and you see the patient's face turn red, and feel trembling on their forehead as if from a shiver; and their eyelids become thin and moist so that the hair of the eyelashes falls out, and the eyelashes are scalded by the heat of the tears, then this treatment is necessary.
