When it is fully dislocated, make the patient sit upright and have an assistant hold their leg above the ankle; pull the foot towards you with your right hand, then twice with your left, extend upwards, and press the foot firmly upwards; do this twice as we have said, pulling and pushing on the foot; if it resets well, but if not, repeat the process, for it will return; if it cannot be reset thus, make the patient lie on their back on the ground, and drive a stout stake into the earth between their thighs, securing cloth around it so as to not injure the patient; then have an assistant hold the thigh, while another extends the foot with their hands or a cord tied above the ankle; each assistant must extend equally, and the stake should be beside the patient's thighs to support them when extended; next, place your hands evenly over the dislocation, while another assistant holds the healthy leg underneath, and the dislocation will return swiftly.
Et quant elle iert a point, si met l’emplastre et estoupes sus, et l’estrain forment, et lie lou piet a la jambe, et warde les ners qui sont sus la cheville derrier, que li liiens ne soit trop estrois; puis le laisse II jors ou III, et se li liiens amolist, si l’estrain; puis le deslie au tier jor ou au quart, et deffent a aler lou malaide par IIII jors; et s’il va devant cel termine, ce n’est mie seurtez qu’il ne desalue encor.	And when it is at the right point, place the plaster and pads on top, apply strong pressure, bind the foot to the leg, and watch over the nerves that are above the ankle behind, ensuring the binding is not too tight; then leave it for two or three days, and if the binding loosens, reapply the strain; afterwards, release the binding on the third or fourth day, and prevent the patient from moving for four days; and if they move before this time, it is not secure that it will not dislocate again.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si covient que tu l’apaises, si com nos avons dit autre part, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if hot abscesses appear there, it is necessary to ease them, as we have said elsewhere, until they are healed.
des dois	twice.
Quant li doi sont desaluez, si les covient bellement estendre sens travail, et c’est legiere chose.	When the thumb is dislocated, one should stretch it gently without strain, and this is a simple matter.
Et se li dislocations est en aucun nout dou dos dou piet, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide sus I leu plain ou sus .ie. table tot droit, et met ton piet sus ce qui apert de ces jointures, puis presse a ton piet forment, tant qu’il reviegne; et quant il est igalz, et il n’i apert nient, si met desoz la plante dou piet une table a II chiés, puis l’estrain forment, et le laisse III jors, puis le deslie; et le fai reposer, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the dislocation is in any nut of the foot or back, you must make the patient sit on a flat surface or on a straight table, and place your foot on what appears to be these joints, then press hard with your foot until it returns; and when it is aligned, and nothing seems amiss, place under the sole of the foot a two-legged table, then strain it forcefully, and leave it there for three days, then release it; and let them rest until they are healed.
de plaie et de dislocation ensamble	Of wounds and dislocations together
Quant plaie vient avec la dislocation, et on la vuet restorer, maintes fois avient que li malaides muert: si ne soies mie presumptuous en la cure, se tu n’es saiges en l’art et tu ne l’as useit longement, et se tu n’es pitous et misericors et tardis, ne mie hardis; et use au comencement de choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et laisse le malaide en la main Deu, se tu n’i vois esperance de santeit; et quant tu i vois esperance, si ramoinne maintenant le membre au leu, ainsois que li apostemes chaus i viegne; et quant li membres est a leu, si aministre choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et cure la plaie, si com il covient, d’oignemens desiccatis; et se avec la dislocation a brisure, et os menus desevrez, si les oste, et fai ce que nos avons dit en maladies simples; et te garde d’entrer en voie de paour, selonc ce que j’ai dit, car ce te vaut mues selonc ton Creator, et por la saveteit de t’arme et de ton cors.	When a wound comes with dislocation and you wish to restore it, often the patient dies: do not be presumptuous in your cure if you are not wise in this art and have not practiced it long, nor uncompassionate or unsympathetic, but bold; use at first soothing ointments for abscesses that are hot, and leave the sick man in God's hands if you see no hope of health; when you see some hope, reset now the limb to its place, despite the fact that heat may come from an abscess; once the limb is back where it belongs, then apply soothing treatments for hot abscesses, and treat the wound as required with drying ointments; and if there was a fracture alongside the dislocation which broke small bones, remove them, and do what we have said in simple illnesses; be careful not to fall into fear according to what I've said, because this will serve you well according to your Creator for the health of your body.
Amen	Amen
